* * *

This is the full workbook for middle school learners with answer keys and lecture notes. Workbook only version and high school versions also available on Amazon.

📘 25x: Introduction to Artificial Intelligence (AI) – Middle School Curriculum (Grades 6–8) 2025–26 Edition

Help Your Students Master AI Literacy, Ethics, and Creative Thinking—One Lesson at a Time

Artificial Intelligence isn’t the future—it’s the present. 25x: Introduction to Artificial Intelligence (AI) is your ready-to-teach, standards-aligned curriculum that equips middle school students to understand, question, and create with AI. With 25 structured, thought-provoking lessons, this workbook empowers students to explore how AI works, where it’s used, how to interact with it effectively, and how to think ethically in an AI-powered world.

✅ You Get:

- 25 Complete Lessons grouped into 5 purposeful units
- Student-Ready Articles written in age-appropriate, engaging language
- Guided Notes + Vocabulary Builders that reinforce comprehension
- Ethical “What If?” Scenarios and problem-solving challenges
- Reflection Questions that foster critical thinking and classroom discussion
- Crosswords, Word Searches, & Extension Activities for reinforcement and fun
- Answer Keys & Lecture Notes for every lesson
- Online Access: Ready-to-teach slide decks, video intros, and AI tutor integration
- Standards Aligned: Meets CCSS, ISTE, and CSTA guidelines

👩🏫 Ideal For:

- Technology & STEM teachers
- Middle school ELA or social studies crossover classes
- Homeschool & hybrid educators
- CTE pathways in AI, computer science, or digital literacy
- Enrichment programs & gifted education
- Parents prepping students for a tech-forward future

Built by educators. Powered by standards. Ready to teach.

📚 Full Table of Contents

Unit 1: Understanding Artificial Intelligence

1\. What is Artificial Intelligence?

2\. How AI Works

3\. AI in Our Daily Lives

4\. The Building Blocks of AI

5\. AI vs. Human Intelligence

Unit 2: Communicating with AI Systems

6\. Understanding AI Communication

7\. Crafting Effective Prompts

8\. Advanced Prompting Techniques

9\. Visual Communication with AI

10\. Evaluating AI Responses

Unit 3: AI Ethics and Responsible Use

11\. AI Bias and Fairness

12\. Privacy and Data

13\. Responsible AI Use at School

14\. AI Safety and Security

15\. Inclusive and Accessible AI

Unit 4: Learning and Creating with AI

16\. AI as a Learning Partner

17\. Research and Information Literacy with AI

18\. Creative Problem-Solving with AI

19\. Digital Storytelling with AI

20\. Building AI-Enhanced Projects

Unit 5: AI and Our Future

21\. Jobs and Careers in an AI World

22\. AI in Different Industries

23\. Human Skills in an AI Era

24\. AI Innovation and Robotics

25\. Becoming AI-Ready Citizens

💡 Whether you're building AI readiness in your classroom or preparing students for a changing digital world, this workbook gives you the tools to do it with confidence.

# Why can't I get these titles?

Under state law, teens need a parent or guardian to buy or borrow titles. Ask your parent or guardian to acquire these titles for this account from their device. These books will appear in your Kindle library once they do.

[**Lee Eyerman**](https://www.amazon.com/Lee-Eyerman/e/B0DB77P3FT/ref=aufs_dp_mata_dsk)

Brief content visible, double tap to read full content.

Full content visible, double tap to read brief content.

Lee is passionate about helping others unlock their full potential by assisting them in discovering their life’s passions and providing guidance to help them meet their goals. Lee believes each of us are beautiful and unique individuals with a grand personal purpose to be fulfilled. He is a lifelong proponent of career and technical education that includes life skills, soft skills, and most importantly, human behavior skills so people are prepared to thrive in adulthood. As an educator, Lee spent over 16 years teaching students career and life skills in order for them to find rewarding careers in the business and technology industries. Prior to teaching, Lee was a corporate attorney working in corporate mergers and acquisitions in NJ and NYC.

Lee holds a Bachelors of Science degree in Business Administration, a Masters of Education in Curriculum and Instruction with an emphasis in Applied Behavior Analysis (ABA) and a Juris Doctor degree in Law. He is retired in good standing from the State of NJ Bar and holds multiple teaching licenses in New York and Idaho.

Lee is excited about developing his mind, body and spirit further as part of the 3andB community.

How customer reviews and ratings work

Customer Reviews, including Product Star Ratings help customers to learn more about the product and decide whether it is the right product for them.

To calculate the overall star rating and percentage breakdown by star, we don’t use a simple average. Instead, our system considers things like how recent a review is and if the reviewer bought the item on Amazon. It also analyzed reviews to verify trustworthiness.

[Learn more how customers reviews work on Amazon](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_omni_lm_btn?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)

##### [_5.0 out of 5 stars_ Never seen learning this fun](https://www.amazon.com/gp/customer-reviews/R13FU7D8XKOGDV/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)



Reviewed in the United States on January 29, 2026

Format: Kindle [Verified Purchase](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_avp?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)






A wonderfully laid out guide for young students to learn and make use of AI. The authors make a very complicated subject sound simple and fun at the same time.

This broad topic is broken down into manageable bites, with succinct sections, each explaining a specific aspect of this amazing technology. Each section builds on the next, giving the student reader a growing understanding of how to best use AI. Guidelines are also given for using it ethically; fact-checking, not cheating or taking academic shortcuts. Good lessons for adults as well!

What is most unique is the use of worksheets after each section, allowing students to grasp the teachings and apply them in practical scenarios. Also, there are puzzles that pertain to the material in each section; a way to keep students interested and let them have a good time with it.

I have to admit that as an adult, I learned a ton from this book. I can’t imagine how this material could have been presented in a more clear, interesting and engaging way. I wish my schoolbooks were this impressive back in my day!









Read more

##### [_5.0 out of 5 stars_ AI concepts finally made clear](https://www.amazon.com/gp/customer-reviews/RNR44SC9MF4VV/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)



Reviewed in the United States on January 23, 2026

Format: Kindle [Verified Purchase](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_avp?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)






I picked this up expecting basics, but it ended up helping me understand artificial intelligence in a way that feels genuinely clear and memorable. The explanations are broken down in a step-by-step way that doesn’t assume you already know everything, which made it much easier to follow. I really appreciated having practice questions with answer keys — they helped reinforce what I was learning and showed me where I needed to review. The lecture notes tied everything together and made the ideas stick instead of just skimming the surface. By the end, I felt more confident, curious, and ready to explore AI with a strong foundation instead of confusion.

##### [_4.0 out of 5 stars_ Excellent, Thorough Materials - Check Compatibiliy, Maybe Buy the Hardcopy Version](https://www.amazon.com/gp/customer-reviews/R271RDB1BFILFV/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)



Reviewed in the United States on November 20, 2025

Format: Kindle [Verified Purchase](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_avp?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)






Kindle Version: This book contains a massive course in the essential aspects of Artificial Intelligence. It contains 25 instructional modules followed by exercises and puzzles that reinforce the concepts. Although most of the book/courses in the 25x series are aimed at the middle school level, this book delves into some areas that are probably best handled at a more mature level although this comprehensive collection gives any monitor or learner many options. Before choosing this Kindle version, it’s important to check that your target device is compatible. A buyer should also be aware that this version does not yet support interoperability, so a student wishing to keep track of learning should probably purchase the hardcopy version rather than the ebook. All-in-all, though, excellent, thorough materials.

##### [_5.0 out of 5 stars_ A thoughtful, engaging, and perfectly age-appropriate AI curriculum.](https://www.amazon.com/gp/customer-reviews/R1FMCXKSNLYMS1/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)

Format: Kindle [Verified Purchase](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_avp?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)






A good introduction to artificial intelligence for middle school kids. This workbook has clear explanations with hands-on learning—featuring guided notes, true/false questions, word searches, and reflection prompts. The 25 lessons progress smoothly from basics to complex topics like AI ethics and safety. Teachers will appreciate the lecture notes, slides, and videos. A thoughtful, engaging, and perfectly age-appropriate AI curriculum.
